=== X → C ===
# {
    ! "Hello World"
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    printf("Hello World\n");
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    ! "Hello World"
}
---
fn main() {
    println!("Hello World");
}

=== X → MOJO ===
# {
    ! "Hello World"
}
---
fn main():
    print("Hello World")

=== X → C ===
# {
    $x = 10
    $y = 20
    ! x + y = 
    ! x + y
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int x = 10;
    int y = 20;
    printf("x + y = %d\n", x + y);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    $x = 10
    $y = 20
    ! x + y = 
    ! x + y
}
---
fn main() {
    let x = 10;
    let y = 20;
    println!("x + y = {}", x + y);
}

=== X → MOJO ===
# {
    $x = 10
    $y = 20
    ! x + y = 
    ! x + y
}
---
fn main():
    let x = 10
    let y = 20
    print("x + y = ", x + y)

=== X → C ===
# {
    @PI = 3.14159
    @MAX = 100
    ! PI = 
    ! @PI
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
#define PI 3.14159
#define MAX 100
int main() {
    printf("PI = %f\n", PI);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    @PI = 3.14159
    @MAX = 100
    ! PI = 
    ! @PI
}
---
const PI: f64 = 3.14159;
const MAX: i32 = 100;
fn main() {
    println!("PI = {}", PI);
}

=== X → MOJO ===
# {
    @PI = 3.14159
    @MAX = 100
    ! PI = 
    ! @PI
}
---
let PI: Float64 = 3.14159
let MAX: Int = 100
fn main():
    print("PI = ", PI)

=== X → C ===
# {
    $name = "XC Language"
    ! name
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    char* name = "XC Language";
    printf("%s\n", name);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    $name = "XC Language"
    ! name
}
---

    let name = "XC Language";
    println!("{}", name);
}

=== X → MOJO ===
# {
    $name = "XC Language"
    ! name
}
---
fn main():
    let name = "XC Language"
    print(name)

=== X → C ===
# {
    $a = 15
    $b = 4
    ! a + b = 
    ! a + b
    ! a - b = 
    ! a - b
    ! a * b = 
    ! a * b
    ! a / b = 
    ! a / b
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int a = 15, b = 4;
    printf("a + b = %d\n", a + b);
    printf("a - b = %d\n", a - b);
    printf("a * b = %d\n", a * b);
    printf("a / b = %d\n", a / b);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    $a = 15
    $b = 4
    ! a + b = 
    ! a + b
    ! a - b = 
    ! a - b
    ! a * b = 
    ! a * b
    ! a / b = 
    ! a / b
}
---
fn main() {
    let a = 15;
    let b = 4;
    println!("a + b = {}", a + b);
    println!("a - b = {}", a - b);
    println!("a * b = {}", a * b);
    println!("a / b = {}", a / b);
}

    print("a / b = ", a // b)

=== X → C ===
# {
    $i = 0
    i = i + 1
    ! ++i = 
    ! i
    i = i - 1
    ! --i = 
    ! i
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int i = 0;
    i++;
    printf("++i = %d\n", i);
    i--;
    printf("--i = %d\n", i);
    return 0;
}

    ! i

    ! i
}

    let mut i = 0;
    i += 1;
    println!("++i = {}", i);
    i -= 1;
    println!("--i = {}", i);
}

int main() {
    int x = 5;
    if (x > 0 && x < 10) printf("x in (0, 10)\n");
    if (x < 0 || x > 100) printf("x out of range\n");
    if (!(x == 5)) printf("x != 5\n");
    return 0;
}

    int grade = 85;
    if (grade >= 90) {
        printf("A\n");
    } else if (grade >= 80) {
        printf("B\n");
    } else if (grade >= 70) {
        printf("C\n");
    } else {
        printf("D\n");
    }
    return 0;
}
---
fn main():
    let grade = 85
    if grade >= 90:
        print("A")
    elif grade >= 80:
        print("B")
    elif grade >= 70:
        print("C")
    else:
        print("D")

=== RUST → X ===
fn main() {
    let grade = 85;
    if grade >= 90 {
        println!("A");
    } else if grade >= 80 {
        println!("B");
    } else if grade >= 70 {
        println!("C");
    } else {
        println!("D");
    }
}
---
# {
    $grade = 85
    ? grade >= 90 {
        ! "A"
    } ?? grade >= 80 {
        ! "B"
    } ?? grade >= 70 {
        ! "C"
    } ?: {
        ! "D"
    }
}

=== RUST → C ===

=== X → C ===
% add(a, b) {
    ^ a + b
}
# {
    $result = add(3, 5)
    ! result
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int add(int a, int b) {
    return a + b;
}
int main() {
    int result = add(3, 5);
    printf("%d\n", result);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===

    ^ a + b
}
# {
    $result = add(3, 5)
    ! result
}

    a + b
}

    let result = add(3, 5);
    println!("{}", result);
}

    print(result)

=== X → C ===
% sum(arr, len) {
    $s = 0
    ~i = 0; i < len; i = i + 1 {
        s = s + arr[i]
    }
    ^ s
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
    ! sum(arr, 5)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int sum(int arr[], int len) {
    int s = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        s += arr[i];
    }
    return s;
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};
    printf("%d\n", sum(arr, 5));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% sum(arr, len) {
    $s = 0
    ~i = 0; i < len; i = i + 1 {
        s = s + arr[i]
    }
    ^ s
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
    ! sum(arr, 5)
}
---
fn sum(arr: &[i32]) -> i32 {
    arr.iter().sum()
}
fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
    println!("{}", sum(&arr));
}

=== X → C ===
% max(arr, len) {
    $m = arr[0]
    ~i = 1; i < len; i = i + 1 {
        ? arr[i] > m {
            m = arr[i]
        }
    }
    ^ m
}
# {
    $arr = [3, 7, 2, 9, 4]
    ! max(arr, 5)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int max(int arr[], int len) {
    int m = arr[0];
    for (int i = 1; i < len; i++) {
        if (arr[i] > m) m = arr[i];
    }
    return m;
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {3, 7, 2, 9, 4};
    printf("%d\n", max(arr, 5));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% max(arr, len) {
    $m = arr[0]
    ~i = 1; i < len; i = i + 1 {

            m = arr[i]
        }
    }
    ^ m

& Point {
    x: Int
    y: Int
}
% distance(p1, p2) {
    $dx = p2.x - p1.x
    $dy = p2.y - p1.y
    ^ (dx*dx + dy*dy) ** 0.5
}
# {
    $p1 = Point { x: 0, y: 0 }
    $p2 = Point { x: 3, y: 4 }
    ! distance(p1, p2)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <math.h>
typedef struct { int x; int y; } Point;
double distance(Point p1, Point p2) {
    int dx = p2.x - p1.x;
    int dy = p2.y - p1.y;
    return sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
}
int main() {
    Point p1 = {0, 0};
    Point p2 = {3, 4};
    printf("%f\n", distance(p1, p2));
    return 0;
}

fn distance(p1: Point, p2: Point) -> f64 {
    let dx = p2.x - p1.x;
    let dy = p2.y - p1.y;
    ((dx*dx + dy*dy) as f64).sqrt()
}
fn main() {
    let p1 = Point { x: 0, y: 0 };
    let p2 = Point { x: 3, y: 4 };

=== X → C ===
% find(arr, len, target) {
    ~i = 0; i < len; i = i + 1 {
        ? arr[i] == target {
            ^ Some(i)
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7]
    $result = find(arr, 4, 5)
    ? result != None {
        ! "Found"
    } ?: {
        ! "Not Found"
    }
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdbool.h>
int* find(int arr[], int len, int target) {
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        if (arr[i] == target) return &arr[i];
    }
    return NULL;
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {1, 3, 5, 7};
    int *result = find(arr, 4, 5);
    if (result != NULL) printf("Found\n");
    else printf("Not Found\n");
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% find(arr, len, target) {
    ~i = 0; i < len; i = i + 1 {
        ? arr[i] == target {
            ^ Some(i)
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7]
    $result = find(arr, 4, 5)
    ? result != None {
        ! "Found"
    } ?: {
        ! "Not Found"
    }
}
---
fn find(arr: &[i32], target: i32) -> Option<usize> {
    arr.iter().position(|&x| x == target)
}
fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 3, 5, 7];
    match find(&arr, 5) {
        Some(i) => println!("Found at {}", i),
        None => println!("Not Found"),
    }
}

=== X → MOJO ===
% find(arr, len, target) {
    ~i = 0; i < len; i = i + 1 {

            ^ Some(i)
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7]

        ! "Found"
    } ?: {
        ! "Not Found"
    }
}
---
fn find(arr: List[Int], target: Int) -> Optional[Int]:
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        if arr[i] == target: return Optional(i)
    return None
fn main():
    let arr = [1, 3, 5, 7]
    let result = find(arr, 5)
    print(result)

#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int arr[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};
    int result = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        if (arr[i] % 2 == 1) {
            result += arr[i] * 2;
        }
    }
    printf("%d\n", result);
    return 0;
}

fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
    let result: i32 = arr.iter()
        .filter(|&&x| x % 2 == 1)
        .map(|&x| x * 2)
        .sum();
    println!("{}", result);
}

int main() {

    int result = 0;

fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
    let result: i32 = arr.iter()
        .filter(|&&x| x % 2 == 1)
        .map(|&x| x * 2)
        .sum();
    println!("{}", result);
}

=== X → C ===
% bubble_sort(arr, n) {
    ~i = 0; i < n - 1; i = i + 1 {
        ~j = 0; j < n - i - 1; j = j + 1 {
            ? arr[j] > arr[j + 1] {
                $tmp = arr[j]
                arr[j] = arr[j + 1]
                arr[j + 1] = tmp
            }
        }
    }
}
# {
    $arr = [64, 34, 25, 12, 22]
    bubble_sort(arr, 5)
    ! arr
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
void bubble_sort(int arr[], int n) {
    for (int i = 0; i < n - 1; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < n - i - 1; j++) {
            if (arr[j] > arr[j + 1]) {
                int tmp = arr[j];
                arr[j] = arr[j + 1];
                arr[j + 1] = tmp;
            }
        }
    }
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {64, 34, 25, 12, 22};
    bubble_sort(arr, 5);
    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) printf("%d ", arr[i]);
    return 0;
}

fn bubble_sort(arr: &mut [i32]) {
    let n = arr.len();
    for i in 0..n {
        for j in 0..n - i - 1 {
            if arr[j] > arr[j + 1] {
                arr.swap(j, j + 1);
            }
        }
    }
}
fn main() {
    let mut arr = vec![64, 34, 25, 12, 22];
    bubble_sort(&mut arr);
    println!("{:?}", arr);
}

=== X → C ===
% binary_search(arr, n, target) {
    $left = 0
    $right = n - 1
    @left <= right {
        $mid = (left + right) / 2
        ? arr[mid] == target {
            ^ Some(mid)
        } ?? arr[mid] < target {
            left = mid + 1
        } ?: {
            right = mid - 1
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11]
    ! binary_search(arr, 6, 7)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int binary_search(int arr[], int n, int target) {
    int left = 0, right = n - 1;
    while (left <= right) {
        int mid = (left + right) / 2;
        if (arr[mid] == target) return mid;
        else if (arr[mid] < target) left = mid + 1;
        else right = mid - 1;
    }
    return -1;
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11};
    printf("%d\n", binary_search(arr, 6, 7));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% binary_search(arr, n, target) {
    $left = 0
    $right = n - 1
    @left <= right {
        $mid = (left + right) / 2
        ? arr[mid] == target {
            ^ Some(mid)
        } ?? arr[mid] < target {
            left = mid + 1
        } ?: {
            right = mid - 1
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11]
    ! binary_search(arr, 6, 7)
}
---
fn binary_search(arr: &[i32], target: i32) -> Option<usize> {
    let mut left = 0;
    let mut right = arr.len();
    while left < right {
        let mid = (left + right) / 2;
        if arr[mid] == target { return Some(mid); }
        else if arr[mid] < target { left = mid + 1; }
        else { right = mid; }
    }
    None
}
fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11];
    println!("{:?}", binary_search(&arr, 7));
}

    $left = 0
    $right = n - 1

        ? arr[mid] == target {
            ^ Some(mid)
        } ?? arr[mid] < target {
            left = mid + 1
        } ?: {
            right = mid - 1
        }
    }
    ^ None
}
# {
    $arr = [1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11]
    ! binary_search(arr, 6, 7)
}
---
fn binary_search(arr: List[Int], target: Int) -> Optional[Int]:
    var left = 0
    var right = len(arr) - 1
    while left <= right:
        let mid = (left + right) // 2
        if arr[mid] == target: return Optional(mid)
        elif arr[mid] < target: left = mid + 1
        else: right = mid - 1
    return None
fn main():
    let arr = [1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11]
    print(binary_search(arr, 7))

        else right = mid - 1;
    }
    return -1;
}
int main() {
    int arr[] = {1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11};
    printf("%d\n", binary_search(arr, 6, 7));
    return 0;
}

=== MOJO → RUST ===
fn binary_search(arr: List[Int], target: Int) -> Optional[Int]:
    var left = 0
    var right = len(arr) - 1
    while left <= right:
        let mid = (left + right) // 2
        if arr[mid] == target: return Optional(mid)
        elif arr[mid] < target: left = mid + 1
        else: right = mid - 1
    return None
fn main():
    let arr = [1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11]
    print(binary_search(arr, 7))
---
fn binary_search(arr: &[i32], target: i32) -> Option<usize> {
    let mut left = 0;
    let mut right = arr.len();
    while left < right {
        let mid = (left + right) / 2;
        if arr[mid] == target { return Some(mid); }
        else if arr[mid] < target { left = mid + 1; }
        else { right = mid; }
    }
    None
}
fn main() {
    let arr = vec![1, 3, 5, 7, 9, 11];
    println!("{:?}", binary_search(&arr, 7));
}

    }
    ^ true

    *err = 0;
    return (double)a / b;

#include <stdio.h>
#include <errno.h>
double divide(int a, int b, int *err) {
    if (b == 0) { *err = 1; return 0; }
    *err = 0;
    return (double)a / b;
}
int main() {
    int err = 0;
    double result = divide(10, 0, &err);
    if (err) printf("division by zero\n");
    else printf("%f\n", result);
    return 0;
}
---
fn divide(a: Int, b: Int) raises -> Int:
    if b == 0: raise Error("division by zero")
    return a // b
fn main():
    try:
        print(divide(10, 0))
    except e:
        print(e)

=== RUST → X ===
fn divide(a: i32, b: i32) -> Result<i32, &'static str> {
    if b == 0 { Err("division by zero") }
    else { Ok(a / b) }
}
fn main() {
    match divide(10, 0) {
        Ok(v) => println!("{}", v),
        Err(e) => println!("{}", e),
    }
}
---
% divide(a, b) {
    ? b == 0 {
        ^ Err("division by zero")
    }
    ^ Ok(a / b)
}
# {
    $result = divide(10, 0)
    ? result.kind == Ok {
        ! result.value
    } ?: {
        ! result.error
    }
}

=== X → C ===
# {
    thread {
        ! "Thread 1"
    }
    thread {
        ! "Thread 2"
    }
    sleep(100)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
#include <pthread.h>
void* thread1(void* arg) {
    printf("Thread 1\n");
    return NULL;
}
void* thread2(void* arg) {
    printf("Thread 2\n");
    return NULL;
}
int main() {
    pthread_t t1, t2;
    pthread_create(&t1, NULL, thread1, NULL);
    pthread_create(&t2, NULL, thread2, NULL);
    pthread_join(t1, NULL);
    pthread_join(t2, NULL);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    thread {
        ! "Thread 1"
    }
    thread {
        ! "Thread 2"
    }
    sleep(100)
}
---
use std::thread;
use std::time::Duration;
fn main() {
    let t1 = thread::spawn(|| { println!("Thread 1"); });
    let t2 = thread::spawn(|| { println!("Thread 2"); });
    thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(100));
    t1.join().unwrap();
    t2.join().unwrap();
}

=== X → C ===
% gcd(a, b) {
    ? b == 0 { ^ a }
    ^ gcd(b, a % b)
}
# {
    ! gcd(48, 18)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int gcd(int a, int b) {
    while (b != 0) { int t = b; b = a % b; a = t; }
    return a;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", gcd(48, 18));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% gcd(a, b) {
    ? b == 0 { ^ a }
    ^ gcd(b, a % b)
}
# {
    ! gcd(48, 18)
}
---
fn gcd(mut a: i32, mut b: i32) -> i32 {
    while b != 0 { let t = b; b = a % b; a = t; }
    a
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", gcd(48, 18));
}

=== X → MOJO ===
% gcd(a, b) {
    ? b == 0 { ^ a }
    ^ gcd(b, a % b)
}
# {
    ! gcd(48, 18)
}
---
fn gcd(a: Int, b: Int) -> Int:
    var x = a
    var y = b
    while y != 0:
        let t = y
        y = x % y
        x = t
    return x
fn main():
    print(gcd(48, 18))

=== X → C ===
% clamp(v, lo, hi) {
    ? v < lo { ^ lo }
    ? v > hi { ^ hi }
    ^ v
}
# {
    ! clamp(150, 0, 100)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int clamp(int v, int lo, int hi) {
    if (v < lo) return lo;
    if (v > hi) return hi;
    return v;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", clamp(150, 0, 100));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% clamp(v, lo, hi) {
    ? v < lo { ^ lo }
    ? v > hi { ^ hi }
    ^ v
}
# {
    ! clamp(150, 0, 100)
}
---
fn clamp(v: i32, lo: i32, hi: i32) -> i32 {
    v.max(lo).min(hi)
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", clamp(150, 0, 100));
}

=== X → MOJO ===
% clamp(v, lo, hi) {
    ? v < lo { ^ lo }
    ? v > hi { ^ hi }
    ^ v
}
# {
    ! clamp(150, 0, 100)
}
---
fn clamp(v: Int, lo: Int, hi: Int) -> Int:
    if v < lo: return lo
    if v > hi: return hi
    return v
fn main():
    print(clamp(150, 0, 100))

=== X → C ===
% count_digits(n) {
    ? n == 0 { ^ 1 }
    $c = 0
    $t = n
    ~j = 0; j < 20; j = j + 1 {
        ? t == 0 { ^ c }
        $c = c + 1
        $t = t / 10
    }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! count_digits(5020)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int count_digits(int n) {
    if (n == 0) return 1;
    int c = 0;
    while (n > 0) { n /= 10; c++; }
    return c;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", count_digits(5020));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===

        ? t == 0 { ^ c }
        $c = c + 1
        $t = t / 10
    }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! count_digits(5020)
}
---
fn count_digits(mut n: i32) -> i32 {
    if n == 0 { return 1; }
    let mut c = 0;
    while n > 0 { n /= 10; c += 1; }
    c
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", count_digits(5020));
}

fn count_digits(n: Int) -> Int:
    if n == 0: return 1

    while x > 0:
        x = x // 10
        c += 1
    return c

    ? pos >= 0 { ^ pos }

    ! pick(-1, 42)
}

    return (pos >= 0) ? pos : neg;

    printf("%d\n", pick(-1, 42));
    return 0;
}

    ^ neg

fn pick(maybe: Option<i32>, neg: i32) -> i32 {
    maybe.unwrap_or(neg)
}

    println!("{}", pick(None, 42));
}

    ^ neg

% get4(a0, a1, a2, a3, i) {
    ? i == 0 { ^ a0 }
    ? i == 1 { ^ a1 }
    ? i == 2 { ^ a2 }
    ? i == 3 { ^ a3 }
    ^ -1
}
# {
    ! get4(10, 20, 30, 40, 10)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int get4(const int *a, int len, int i) {
    if (i < 0 || i >= len) return -1;
    return a[i];
}
int main() {
    int a[] = {10, 20, 30, 40};
    printf("%d\n", get4(a, 4, 10));
    return 0;
}

    ^ -1
}

    a.get(i).copied()
}

#include <stdio.h>
size_t slen(const char *s) {
    size_t n = 0;
    while (s[n]) n++;
    return n;
}

    return 0;

=== X → C ===
% fact(n) {
    $r = 1
    ~k = 2; k <= n; k = k + 1 {
        $r = r * k
    }
    ^ r
}
# {
    ! fact(6)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int fact(int n) {
    int r = 1;
    for (int k = 2; k <= n; k++) r *= k;
    return r;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", fact(6));
    return 0;
}

=== X → C ===
% modpow(b, e, m) {
    $r = 1
    $x = b % m
    $ee = e
    ~k = 0; ee > 0; k = k + 1 {
        ? ee % 2 == 1 { $r = (r * x) % m }
        $ee = ee / 2
        $x = (x * x) % m
    }
    ^ r
}
# {
    ! modpow(3, 4, 17)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
long modpow(long b, long e, long m) {
    long r = 1 % m;
    b %= m;
    while (e > 0) {
        if (e & 1) r = (r * b) % m;
        b = (b * b) % m;
        e >>= 1;
    }
    return r;
}
int main() {
    printf("%ld\n", modpow(3, 4, 17));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% modpow(b, e, m) {
    $r = 1
    $x = b % m
    $ee = e
    ~k = 0; ee > 0; k = k + 1 {
        ? ee % 2 == 1 { $r = (r * x) % m }
        $ee = ee / 2
        $x = (x * x) % m
    }
    ^ r
}
# {
    ! modpow(3, 4, 17)
}
---
fn modpow(mut b: i64, mut e: i64, m: i64) -> i64 {
    let mut r = 1 % m;
    b %= m;
    while e > 0 {
        if e & 1 == 1 { r = r * b % m; }
        b = b * b % m;
        e >>= 1;
    }
    r
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", modpow(3, 4, 17));
}

    $x = b % m
    $ee = e
    ~k = 0; ee > 0; k = k + 1 {

# {

}
---
fn modpow(b: Int, e: Int, m: Int) -> Int:
    var r = 1 % m
    var x = b % m
    var ee = e
    while ee > 0:
        if ee % 2 == 1:
            r = (r * x) % m
        x = (x * x) % m
        ee = ee // 2
    return r
fn main():
    print(modpow(3, 4, 17))

    while (e > 0) {
        if (e & 1) r = (r * b) % m;
        b = (b * b) % m;
        e >>= 1;
    }
    return r;
}
int main() {
    printf("%ld\n", modpow(3, 4, 17));
    return 0;
}

=== RUST → MOJO ===
fn modpow(mut b: i64, mut e: i64, m: i64) -> i64 {
    let mut r = 1 % m;
    b %= m;
    while e > 0 {
        if e & 1 == 1 { r = r * b % m; }
        b = b * b % m;
        e >>= 1;
    }
    r
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", modpow(3, 4, 17));
}
---
fn modpow(b: Int, e: Int, m: Int) -> Int:
    var r = 1 % m
    var x = b % m
    var ee = e
    while ee > 0:
        if ee % 2 == 1:
            r = (r * x) % m
        x = (x * x) % m
        ee = ee // 2
    return r
fn main():
    print(modpow(3, 4, 17))

    $x = b % m
    $ee = e

        ? ee % 2 == 1 { $r = (r * x) % m }

fn modpow(mut b: i64, mut e: i64, m: i64) -> i64 {
    let mut r = 1 % m;
    b %= m;
    while e > 0 {
        if e & 1 == 1 { r = r * b % m; }
        b = b * b % m;
        e >>= 1;
    }
    r
}

#include <stdio.h>
int second(const int *a, int n) {
    int m1 = a[0] > a[1] ? a[0] : a[1];
    int m2 = a[0] + a[1] - m1;
    for (int i = 2; i < n; i++) {
        if (a[i] >= m1) { m2 = m1; m1 = a[i]; }
        else if (a[i] > m2) m2 = a[i];
    }
    return m2;
}
int main() {
    int a[] = {1, 5, 9, 7};
    printf("%d\n", second(a, 4));
    return 0;
}

fn second(a: List[Int]) -> Int:
    var m1 = a[0]
    var m2 = a[0]
    for i in range(len(a)):
        let v = a[i]
        if v >= m1:
            m2 = m1
            m1 = v
        elif v > m2:
            m2 = v
    return m2

fn absdiff(a: Int, b: Int) -> Int:
    if a > b:
        return a - b
    return b - a

    print(absdiff(3, 10))

    }

=== X → C ===
% safe_mul(a, b, limit) {
    ? a > 0 && b > 0 && a > limit / b { ^ 0 }
    ^ 1
}
# {
    ? safe_mul(1000, 1000, 500000) { ! 1 } ?: { ! 0 }
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int safe_mul(int a, int b, int limit) {
    long long p = (long long)a * b;
    return p <= limit;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", safe_mul(1000, 1000, 500000));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% safe_mul(a, b, limit) {
    ? a > 0 && b > 0 && a > limit / b { ^ 0 }
    ^ 1
}
# {
    ? safe_mul(1000, 1000, 500000) { ! 1 } ?: { ! 0 }
}
---
fn safe_mul(a: i32, b: i32, limit: i32) -> bool {
    match a.checked_mul(b) {
        Some(p) => p <= limit,
        None => false,
    }
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", if safe_mul(1000, 1000, 500000) { 1 } else { 0 });
}

=== X → MOJO ===

}

fn safe_mul(a: Int, b: Int, limit: Int) -> Bool:
    return a * b <= limit

    print(1 if safe_mul(1000, 1000, 500000) else 0)

    if (n < 0) return -1;
    return 0;

    printf("%d\n", sign(-9));
    return 0;
}

    let b = 8;
    println!("{}", (a + b) / 2);

    return (a + b) // 2

=== X → C ===
% pop4(n) {
    $c = 0
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! pop4(13)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int pop4(unsigned n) {
    int c = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) { c += n & 1; n >>= 1; }
    return c;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", pop4(13));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% pop4(n) {
    $c = 0
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    $n = n / 2
    ? n % 2 == 1 { $c = c + 1 }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! pop4(13)
}
---
fn main() {
    println!("{}", (13u8).count_ones());

    ^ c

fn pop4(n: Int) -> Int:
    var c = 0
    var x = n
    for _ in range(4):
        c += x % 2
        x = x // 2
    return c

    print(pop4(13))

=== X → C ===
% max3(a, b, c) {
    $m = a
    ? b > m { $m = b }
    ? c > m { $m = c }
    ^ m
}
# {
    ! max3(2, 9, 5)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int a = 2, b = 9, c = 5;
    int m = a > b ? a : b;
    m = m > c ? m : c;
    printf("%d\n", m);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% max3(a, b, c) {
    $m = a
    ? b > m { $m = b }
    ? c > m { $m = c }
    ^ m
}
# {
    ! max3(2, 9, 5)
}
---
fn main() {
    let m = *[2, 9, 5].iter().max().unwrap();
    println!("{}", m);
}

=== X → MOJO ===
% max3(a, b, c) {
    $m = a
    ? b > m { $m = b }
    ? c > m { $m = c }
    ^ m
}
# {
    ! max3(2, 9, 5)
}
---
fn max3(a: Int, b: Int, c: Int) -> Int:
    var m = a
    if b > m: m = b
    if c > m: m = c
    return m
fn main():
    print(max3(2, 9, 5))

=== X → C ===
% log2f(n) {
    $c = 0
    $x = n
    @x > 1 {
        $x = x / 2
        $c = c + 1
    }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! log2f(10)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int log2f(unsigned n) {
    int c = 0;
    while (n > 1) { n >>= 1; c++; }
    return c;
}
int main() {
    printf("%d\n", log2f(10));
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
% log2f(n) {
    $c = 0
    $x = n
    @x > 1 {
        $x = x / 2
        $c = c + 1
    }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! log2f(10)
}
---
fn log2f(mut n: u32) -> u32 {
    let mut c = 0;
    while n > 1 { n >>= 1; c += 1; }
    c
}
fn main() {
    println!("{}", log2f(10));
}

=== X → MOJO ===

    $x = n
    @x > 1 {
        $x = x / 2
        $c = c + 1
    }
    ^ c
}
# {
    ! log2f(10)
}
---
fn log2f(n: Int) -> Int:
    var c = 0
    var x = n
    while x > 1:
        x = x // 2
        c += 1
    return c
fn main():
    print(log2f(10))

fn log2f(mut n: u32) -> u32 {
    let mut c = 0;
    while n > 1 { n >>= 1; c += 1; }
    c

# {
    $x: int = -1
    ? ((x > 0)) {
        ◎O "pos"
    } ?: {
        ◎O "nonpos"
    }
}

#include <stdio.h>
int main() {

    if (x > 0) puts("pos");

#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
int main() {
    const char* s = "abc";
    printf("%zu\n", strlen(s));
    return 0;
}
---
fn main() {
    let s = "abc";
    println!("{}", s.len());
}

=== C → MOJO ===
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
int main() {
    const char* s = "abc";
    printf("%zu\n", strlen(s));
    return 0;
}
---
fn main():
    let s = "abc"
    print(len(s))

=== RUST → X ===
fn main() {
    let s = "abc";
    println!("{}", s.len());
}
---
# {
    $s: string = "abc"
    ◎O µN(s)
}

=== RUST → C ===
fn main() {
    let s = "abc";
    println!("{}", s.len());
}

    $port: int = 8080
    ◎O ≈L(port)
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int port = 8080;
    printf("listen stub %d\n", port);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    $port: int = 8080
    ◎O ≈L(port)
}
---

    let port: u16 = 8080;
    println!("listen stub {}", port);
}

=== X → C ===
# {
    $i: int = 0
    ~ j = 0; (j < 10); j = j + 1 {
        $i = i + 1
        ? ((j == 2)) {
            <
        }
        ? ((j == 5)) {
            >
        }
    }
    ◎O i
}
---
#include <stdio.h>
int main() {
    int i = 0;
    for (int j = 0; j < 10; j++) {
        i++;
        if (j == 2) continue;
        if (j == 5) break;
    }
    printf("%d\n", i);
    return 0;
}

=== X → RUST ===
# {
    $i: int = 0
    ~ j = 0; (j < 10); j = j + 1 {
        $i = i + 1
        ? ((j == 2)) {
            <
        }
        ? ((j == 5)) {
            >
        }
    }
    ◎O i
}
---
fn main() {
    let mut i: i32 = 0;
    for j in 0..10 {
        i += 1;
        if j == 2 { continue; }
        if j == 5 { break; }
    }
    println!("{}", i);
}

=== X → MOJO ===
# {

            <
        }
        ? ((j == 5)) {
            >
        }
    }
    ◎O i
}
---
fn main():
    var i = 0
    for j in range(10):
        i += 1
        if j == 2:
            continue
        if j == 5:
            break
    print(i)
